[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing run of the `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` harness against Apache [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s untar functionality triggered a critical security issue: a file path [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal vulnerability. During extraction, an archive entry path containing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal sequences led to writing outside the intended directory [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m[39m…[0m[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the built-in FilePathTraversal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer in Jazzer raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue observed:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer invoked `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`, which calls [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on a generated test case.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - During untarring, an archive entry path containing `..` or absolute elements [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaused files to be extracted outside the sandbox.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal.check` hook detected that the output path [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp9751851135859075633/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` traverses [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupwards from the intended directory.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - A `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal` exception was thrown, terminating the run with exit status [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - File path traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: untrusted archive entries manipulating extraction[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The harness initializes Jazzer sanitizers and instrumentation across Apache [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika, Commons Compress, and Commons IO classes, indicating full coverage of the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntar path.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The relevant sanitizer hook is `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, invoked [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin `[0m[1;35mTikaUntar.main[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The stack trace shows the failure occurs before any custom harness logic beyond[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoking TikaUntar.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer’s reproducer generator produced both a libFuzzer crashing input [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive and a Java reproducer.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `com.example.TikaAppUntarringFuzzer` – the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry point for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar` – the CLI utility for untarring archives.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Underlying extraction logic in Apache Commons Compress:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveInputStream`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.ArchiveEntry` and related classes[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Path handling utilities in Apache Commons IO, such as [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.io.FileUtils` or `org.apache.commons.io.file.PathUtils`, which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmay normalize or resolve entry paths.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer implementation for understanding the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexact path validation logic.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese components together form the untar pipeline and should be reviewed to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand how malicious entry names bypass or trigger path traversal checks, and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure extraction is safely sandboxed.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m:import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m:import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveInputStream;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:33[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m41[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:    public static void [0m[1;35mmain[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m args[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:                TarArchiveInputStream tais = new [0m[1;35mTarArchiveInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:            TarArchiveEntry tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:            while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m49[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:            while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:                    Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:                tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m49[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:            while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:                    Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:                tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The vulnerability arises because malicious `TarArchiveEntry` names containing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading “..” segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor absolute paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are resolved and normalized to paths [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside the intended extraction directory. The current patch throws an [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` when such traversal is detected, but this exception propagates out of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`main`, causing the fuzzer harness to treat it as a crash [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We need [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto prevent both the actual path‐traversal write and any exception propagation for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthese entries, while preserving normal extraction behavior for safe entries.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Insights from Code Snippets  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The extraction directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`extractDir`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must be normalized once at startup.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inside the loop, each entry’s target path is computed via [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The risky part is calling file-system APIs [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Files.createDirectories` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Files.write`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on the normalized `target`, which triggers the sanitizer/harness on [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsafe paths.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throwing an exception to abort on detection will always bubble out of `main`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashing the harness.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Normalize the extraction directory immediately upon reading the argument, as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the previous patch:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `Path extractDir = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39margs[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. In the loop over `TarArchiveEntry` objects, *do not throw* on detecting a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath traversal. Instead:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Detect unsafe entries by checking `![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Log a warning to `System.err` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso users/operators know an entry was [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Skip** any write or directory‐creation calls for unsafe entries.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Continue processing the remaining entries normally. Do **not** let any [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath‐traversal incidents escape as exceptions from `main`.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Preserve the existing exception signature [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`throws IOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that real[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI/O errors still surface, but traversal‐specific errors no longer trigger a harness[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `TikaUntar.main`, change the extraction-directory normalization [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdone in prior patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the traversal‐check block inside the loop:  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Instead of throwing IOException, log and skip:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping unsafe entry: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove the `throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` lines that were added in the last [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch attempt.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Leave all other logic unchanged: safe entries are unaltered, and true I/O [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disk full, malformed stream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will still raise exceptions and abort [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No harness or fuzzing‐logic changes:** The skip approach leaves the harness [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched and avoids crash conditions.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Core extraction logic intact:** Safe entries are extracted exactly as [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No broad exception catching:** Only the malicious‐entry scenario is handled;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgenuine I/O errors still bubble up.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Clear diagnostics:** Warnings on `System.err` inform users of skipped [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries without terminating the CLI with an error code.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - CLI exit code on encountering malicious entries will now be `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msuccess[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. If [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream scripts rely on non‐zero exit codes for any invalid entry, they will [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneed to parse stderr. However, most users prefer skipping unsafe entries silently [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than abrupt abort.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging to stderr should not break existing automated tests unless they [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly validate error output. Empirical review shows no existing tests for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath‐traversal behavior.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Reference Code Ranges  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:41[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m49[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcod[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95me_range[0m[39m>  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m([0m[39mThis is where the loop and the traversal check occur.[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImplementing this strategy ensures that path-traversal attempts no longer result in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man unhandled exception and crash, while preserving the intended extraction [0m         [2m                [0m
